Vive/Rift: Click Menu/B/Y Button to activate locomotion on a hand. Primary 2axis inputs behave like a gamepad (and cannot use weapon functions while active). \n\nIndex/WMR: Joysticks behave like gamepad.\n\nNOTE: There is NO smooth turning available.\n\nGravity & Wall Collision are Enabled.=Vive/Rift：单击菜单/B/Y按钮激活这支手的移动控制。主要2轴输入的行为类似于游戏手柄（并且在激活时无法使用武器功能）。\n\nIndex/WMR：摇杆的行为类似于游戏手柄。\n\n注意：无法使用平滑转向。\n\n重力和墙壁碰撞已启用。
Click Menu/B/Y Button to activate locomotion on a hand. This hand now moves you (and cannot use weapon functions while active).\n\nPress primary 2axis input (touchpad/joystick) forward/up and hold.\n\nDrag input to the side to make arrow at end of arc turn. Release input to teleport.\n\nGravity & Wall Collision are Disabled=单击菜单/B/Y按钮激活这支手的移动控制。这只手现在会移动你（而且激活时无法使用武器功能）。\n\n向前/向上按下主要2轴输入（触摸板/操纵杆）并按住。\n\n将输入拖到一侧可使弧线末端的箭头转动。释放输入即可传送。\n\n重力和墙壁碰撞已禁用
Click-Hold Menu/B/Y Buttons while swinging that controller (in any direction) to increase speed.\n\nThe direction your controller is pointed controls which way you go. If you hold both controller buttons the direction is averaged. \n\nPunching both hands upward while holding buttons is jump!\n\nGravity & Wall Collision are Disabled=按住菜单/B/Y按钮并摆动控制器（朝任意方向）可提高速度。\n\n控制器指向的方向控制着你的前进方向。如果你同时按住两个控制器按钮，则方向会取平均。\n\n按住按钮的同时双手向上挥动就能跳跃！\n\n重力和墙壁碰撞已禁用

Greetings!\n\nIf you're new to H3, click through the entries on the left there to get a quick start on things, or click a section on the top bar to spawn some toys to play with!\n\nIf you need help with something there are several helpful links to the left, clicking on them will copy the url to your clip board, which you can paste into a web browser to find more info, or join one of our helpful communities!\n\nAll of us here at RUST LTD. hope you have a Wonderful time!=欢迎！\n\n如果你是H3新手，请点击左侧的条目快速上手，或点击顶栏上的一个部分来生成一些玩具来玩！\n\n如果你需要帮助，左侧有几个有用的链接，点击它们会将URL复制到你的剪贴板，你可以将其粘贴到浏览器中以查找更多信息，或者加入我们的乐于助人的社区之一！\n\nRUST LTD的全体同仁希望你度过愉快的时光！

Click on Top Bar buttons to go to their various pages.\r\n\nEach page will save your selection and tags until you load into a different scene or reload the current scene.\r\n\nThis Spawner is still under construction so some pages may be incomplete or missing.\r=单击顶部栏按钮可转到其各个页面。\r\n\n每个页面都会保存你的选择和标签，直到你加载到不同的场景或重新加载当前场景。\r\n\n此生成器仍在建设中，因此某些页面可能不完整或缺失。\r
Click on the FIREARMS button on the Top Bar.\r\n\nUse the Tag categories section on the left to narrow things down.\r\n\nClick on Gun icons to select them, then, in the right most panel, click the SPAWN button and your gun will appear.\r\n=点击顶部栏上的“枪支”按钮。\r\n\n使用左侧的标签类别部分缩小范围。\r\n\n点击枪支图标进行选择，然后在最右侧面板中点击“生成”按钮，你的枪支就会出现。\r\n
You can Click the SPAWN AMMO PANEL button right on this page.\n\nYou can also click on the AMMO button on the Top Bar to see all Ammo, Magazines, Speedloaders and Stripper Clips available in game.\r\n\nThe Ammo page uses similar Tag sorting to Firearms.\r\r=你可以单击此页面上的“生成弹药面板”按钮。\n\n你还可以单击顶部栏上的“弹药”按钮查看游戏中所有可用的弹药、弹匣、快速装弹器和弹夹。\r\n\n弹药页面使用与枪支类似的标签排序。\r\r
You can SPAWNLOCK ammo, magazines, speedloaders, and clips.\r\n1. Place the object in one of your Quickbelt slots.\r\n2. Hover your empty hand over the slot.\r\n3. Click the B button, the slot will turn blue.\r\n4. You can now take copies of that object out of the slot.\r\n5. Check the HELP section for more detailed Spawnlocking mechanics.\r\n=你可以锁定生成弹药、弹匣、快速装弹器和弹夹。\r\n1. 将物体放入你的快捷腰带插槽之一。\r\n2. 将空手悬停在插槽上。\r\n3. 单击B按钮，插槽将变为蓝色。\r\n4. 你现在可以从插槽中复制该物体。\r\n5. 查看帮助部分以获取更详细的锁定生成机制。\r\n
Pretty much all guns shoot by pulling the trigger.\r\nYou might have to do something else first to ready the gun though.\r\nMake sure if your gun has a safety it is disengaged.\r\nThis is done by clicking the B button. You should hear a click.\r\nAlso make sure you've got a round chambered!\r\nVisit the Sample Platter scene for an Intro to common gun controls.\r=几乎所有枪支都是通过扣动扳机来射击的。\r\n不过，你可能必须先做些其他事情来准备好枪支。\r\n如果你的枪支有保险装置，确保保险装置已解除。\r\n这可以通过按下B按钮来完成。你应该会听到咔嗒声。\r\n同时确保你已经装好子弹！\r\n访问“样本拼盘”场景，了解常见枪支控制的介绍。\r
Turn your controller around on an empty hand.\r\n\nThe WRIST MENU should appear.\r\n\nPoint at the 'Options Panel' button with your other controller and click.\r\n\nThis will spawn the Options Panel into your hand.\r=将空手的控制器转动。\r\n\n腕上菜单应该会出现。\r\n\n使用另一个控制器指向“选项面板”按钮并单击。\r\n\n这将在你的手中生成选项面板。\r

New H3VR Scope System Test\n\nGreetings! This Alpha Cycle (Update 113) is about testing a whole system replacement for Magnified Optics. This system:\n\nNew This Week:\n- PHYSICAL SCOPE CONTROLS\n- Lateral View Parallax Simulation\n- Over 20 Scopes brought over to new system\n\n- Auto-culls to a single scope view active at once to ensure more reliable performance overhead\n- Enables correct magnification and field of view for all scopes; Allows for true 1x scopes\r\n- Enables correct reticles with accurate holds and drop compensation\r\n- Correct FFP/SFP behavior\r\n- Approximately physically accurate exit pupil/"eyebox" behavior and eye relief, with optional settings for easier usage\r\n- Allows for 2-eye aiming (ie. ACOG's "Bindon aiming concept" for finding targets at high magnification, or red-dot like behavior with 1x scopes)\r\n- Accurate zeroing using real world units, with moving turrets when applicable\r\n- Adjustable illumination and reticle color with moving turrets when applicable, swappable reticles\r\n- Ability to look through both ends of scopes (though probably not 100% optically correct lol)\r\n- Ability to simulate odd scope behaviors to better emulate certain scopes (lens distortion, chromatic aberration, FOV tunneling, exit pupil offset)\r\n- Data driven, relatively simple setup if you have an accurate model and know it's specs\n=新的 H3VR Scope System Test\n\nGreetings! This Alpha Cycle (更新 113) is about testing a whole system replacement for Magnified Optics. This system:\n\n新的 This Week:\n- PHYSICAL SCOPE CONTROLS\n- Lateral View Parallax Simulation\n- Over 20 Scopes brought over to new system\n\n- Auto-culls to a single scope view active at once to ensure more reliable performance overhead\n- Enables correct magnification and field of view for all scopes; Allows for true 1x scopes\r\n- Enables correct reticles with accurate holds and drop compensation\r\n- Correct FFP/SFP behavior\r\n- Approximately physically accurate exit pupil/"eyebox" behavior and eye relief, with optional settings for easier usage\r\n- Allows for 2-eye aiming (ie. ACOG's "Bindon aiming concept" for finding targets at high magnification, or red-dot like behavior with 1x scopes)\r\n- Accurate zeroing using real world units, with moving turrets when applicable\r\n- Adjustable illumination and reticle color with moving turrets when applicable, swappable reticles\r\n- Ability to look through both ends of scopes (though probably not 100% optically correct lol)\r\n- Ability to simulate odd scope behaviors to better emulate certain scopes (lens distortion, chromatic aberration, FOV tunneling, exit pupil offset)\r\n- Data driven, relatively simple setup if you have an accurate model and know it's specs\n
